\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
A version of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_read_only_chassis_model}{Read\+Only\+Chassis\+Model}} that also supports write methods, such as setting motor speed. Because this class can write to motors, there can only be one owner and as such copying is disabled.

\index{okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}!curvature@{curvature}}
\index{curvature@{curvature}!okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{curvature()}{curvature()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Model\+::curvature (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{iforward\+Speed,  }\item[{double}]{icurvature,  }\item[{double}]{ithreshold = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Drive the robot with a curvature drive layout. The robot drives in constant radius turns where you control the curvature (inverse of radius) you drive in. This is advantageous because the forward speed will not affect the rate of turning. The algorithm switches to arcade if the forward speed is 0. Uses voltage mode.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em iforward\+Speed} & speed in the forward direction \\
\hline
{\em icurvature} & curvature (inverse of radius) to drive in \\
\hline
{\em ithreshold} & deadband on joystick values \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model_a2459ac1128c26c5911fa1696bd185c63}\label{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model_a2459ac1128c26c5911fa1696bd185c63}} 
\index{okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}!curvature@{curvature}}
\index{curvature@{curvature}!okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{curvature()}{curvature()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [6/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Model\+::curvature (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{iforward\+Speed,  }\item[{double}]{icurvature,  }\item[{double}]{ithreshold = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Drive the robot with a curvature drive layout. The robot drives in constant radius turns where you control the curvature (inverse of radius) you drive in. This is advantageous because the forward speed will not affect the rate of turning. The algorithm switches to arcade if the forward speed is 0. Uses voltage mode.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em iforward\+Speed} & speed in the forward direction \\
\hline
{\em icurvature} & curvature (inverse of radius) to drive in \\
\hline
{\em ithreshold} & deadband on joystick values \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Implemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_h_drive_model_adb6f15eb2635677962f1c870d4072430}{okapi\+::\+HDrive\+Model}}, \doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{driveVector()}{driveVector()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [6/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Model\+::drive\+Vector (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{iforward\+Speed,  }\item[{double}]{iyaw }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Drive the robot in an arc (using open-\/loop control). Uses velocity mode. The algorithm is (approximately)\+: left\+Power = forward\+Speed + yaw right\+Power = forward\+Speed -\/ yaw

\index{okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}!driveVectorVoltage@{driveVectorVoltage}}
\index{driveVectorVoltage@{driveVectorVoltage}!okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{driveVectorVoltage()}{driveVectorVoltage()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [6/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Model\+::drive\+Vector\+Voltage (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{iforward\+Speed,  }\item[{double}]{iyaw }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Drive the robot in an arc. Uses voltage mode. The algorithm is (approximately)\+: left\+Power = forward\+Speed + yaw right\+Power = forward\+Speed -\/ yaw


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em iforwad\+Speed} & speed in the forward direction \\
\hline
{\em iyaw} & speed around the vertical axis \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}!setMaxVelocity@{setMaxVelocity}}
\index{setMaxVelocity@{setMaxVelocity}!okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMaxVelocity()}{setMaxVelocity()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Model\+::set\+Max\+Velocity (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{imax\+Velocity }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets a new maximum velocity in RPM. The usable maximum depends on the maximum velocity of the currently installed gearset. If the configured maximum velocity is greater than the attainable maximum velocity from the currently installed gearset, the \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model}{Chassis\+Model}} will still scale to that velocity.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em imax\+Velocity} & The new maximum velocity. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model_ae7fcb4cc95fdd7fd3c8f8388b4a698b2}\label{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model_ae7fcb4cc95fdd7fd3c8f8388b4a698b2}} 
\index{okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}!setMaxVelocity@{setMaxVelocity}}
\index{setMaxVelocity@{setMaxVelocity}!okapi::ChassisModel@{okapi::ChassisModel}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMaxVelocity()}{setMaxVelocity()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [5/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void okapi\+::\+Chassis\+Model\+::set\+Max\+Velocity (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{imax\+Velocity }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets a new maximum velocity in RPM. The usable maximum depends on the maximum velocity of the currently installed gearset. If the configured maximum velocity is greater than the attainable maximum velocity from the currently installed gearset, the \mbox{\hyperlink{classokapi_1_1_chassis_model}{Chassis\+Model}} will still scale to that velocity.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em imax\+Velocity} & The new maximum velocity. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
